SELECT search_id AS up_id, ra AS up_ra, dec AS up_dec   FROM MyDB.FIRCAT_pos  CREATE TABLE #tmp ( 	up_id int, 	objid bigint ) INSERT INTO #tmp  EXEC spGetNeighbors #      INSERT INTO MyDB.tmp9  SELECT DISTINCT MIN(tmp.up_id) AS up_id, tmp.objid AS objid FROM #tmp tmp 	LEFT OUTER JOIN MyDB.tmp7       tmp7 ON tmp7.objid    = tmp.objid 	LEFT OUTER JOIN MyDB.tmp8       tmp8 ON tmp8.objid    = tmp.objid 	LEFT OUTER JOIN MyDB.tmp9       tmp9 ON tmp9.objid    = tmp.objid 	INNER JOIN      DR1#.PhotoPrimary po ON po.objid      = tmp.objid 	LEFT OUTER JOIN DR1#.Photoz       pz ON pz.objid      = po.objid 	LEFT OUTER JOIN DR1#.SpecObj      sp ON sp.bestobjid  = po.objid 	LEFT OUTER JOIN DR1#.WISE_xmatch  wx ON wx.sdss_objid = po.objid 	LEFT OUTER JOIN DR1#.WISE_allsky  wa ON wa.cntr       = wx.wise_cntr 	LEFT OUTER JOIN DR1#.TwoMassXSC   tm ON tm.objid      = po.objid 	LEFT OUTER JOIN DR1#.FIRST        ft ON ft.objid      = po.objid WHERE   	( po.clean = #  	OR ( 		((po.flags & #) != #)         		AND ((po.flags & #) = #)  		                                       		                                       		                                       		                                       		                                       		                                       		AND (((po.flags & #) = #) OR (po.psfmagerr_g <= #)) 		         		         		AND (((po.flags & #) = #) OR (po.flags & #) = #) 		         		         		) 	) 	 	 	AND (po.calibStatus_i & #) != # 	 	 	AND po.cmodelmagerr_i <= #  	 	AND wx.wise_cntr IS NULL 	AND tmp7.up_id IS NULL 	AND tmp8.up_id IS NULL 	AND tmp9.up_id IS NULL 	 	 	 	 	 	     GROUP BY tmp.objid ORDER BY up_id, objid
